###  Kuutonen₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Kuutonen* (six)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  38
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
* Semantic tags:  MEDIA
